The Sock Industry Labor-Capital Dispute Expands The sock industry labor-capital dispute in this county

has been dragging on for three months. Although the county government has repeatedly ordered both sides to abide by the agreement, the capital's attitude is adamant, causing a general workers

to repeatedly petition the party and government authorities. Yesterday was the day for Zhonghua Sock Factory to pay wages again. Worker Fang Xue specially invited union members to supervise. However, when the factory paid the wages, it still did not comply with the agreement. Therefore, the workers questioned them. Jin Zhaolin and others, members of the union's standing committee, were afraid of a dispute and immediately persuaded the workers. On one hand, they asked Factory Owner Ge Ziqi to go to the county for instructions in order to resolve the issue. However, Ge Ziqi expressed his unwillingness, and a dispute arose between the two sides. The police officer at the post reported it and took them to the Fourth Public Security Branch and sent them to the General Bureau. Section Chief Wang opened a court to hear the case. Since the matter had been mediated by the county government, he ordered both parties to wait quietly for the handling. The workers were extremely angry after hearing this news. More than 300 workers from the factory gathered at the General Labor Union to hold a temporary meeting to discuss how to deal with the situation. Wang Ciqing of the County Party Department and Xie Bin of the Workers' Organizations Guidance Office attended to provide guidance and earnestly persuaded them, and the workers dispersed. At the same time, Ji Zhi, Wu Shaoji, Ye Qiaoyun, and other members of the Standing Committee of the Silk Industry Labor Union also sent letters to various labor unions, requesting their unanimous support.

The Thief Who Committed Robbery in Tianshang City Has Been Arrested Yang Yu-feng's Cao workshop, and Ren A-chuan and Ren Shi-fang's families, villagers in Chengxiang Shang Township, under Shigu Bridge, Tangtou Township, Fifth District (Tianshang City) of the county, were robbed by bandits in July, suffering heavy losses. and immediately ordered Xue Fu-rui, captain of the detective team, to conduct a strict investigation and solve the case within a time limit. After receiving the order, Captain Xue immediately transferred the order to all detectives

to cooperate in the arrest. The detective team leader Zai Shou-quan, Shen Hua, and others learned that Yang A-gen, a thief who participated in the robbery, was hiding in the countryside. Yesterday, they presented a document to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Cutting the Scrotum to Commit Suicide Qian Arong, a villager near Hongshengli, Eleventh District (Nanshi City), had a son ten years ago who was blind. He repeatedly sought medical treatment, but there was no effect, and he had spent more than 300 yuan. Therefore, he has been heavily in debt over the years. Recently, Arong became ill due to worry and could not eat. His nerves were disturbed all day long, like a madman. A few days ago, when his wife was not in the room, Arong took a razor and cut his own scrotum. At that time, both testicles drooped down, blood was dripping, and he fell on the bed. Later, his wife noticed it and immediately hired a boat to take him to Suzhou Hospital for treatment. His life is in danger.

Raping a Young Girl, Detained in Court for Interrogation Bian Jinlong, a tailor from the workshop in Nian Wujian Head, Xiaomu Bridge, outside the West Gate of Xiyi,

raped A'er, an eight-year-old girl who lived with him, on the 23rd of last month and then disappeared. Afterwards, Jiang Xingzhu, A'er's aunt, reported the case to the Fourth Branch, and Bian Jinren, Jinlong's elder brother, was detained and sent to the court. Prosecutor Zhou ordered Jinren to be released on bail

and to search for his younger brother and bring him to justice. It is now known that Bian Jinren found his brother Jinlong yesterday and sent him to the court. The plaintiff, Jiang Xingzhu, was summoned to court by the court. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Zhou opened the court for investigation again.

As a result, Jiang Xingzhu was ordered to return, Bian Jinlong was detained, and Bian Jinren was released on bail.

Summary of Three Robbery Cases: Dabeizi Bridge in Dongtang City, Hengtang District, is a crucial thoroughfare on the Kun-Chang shipping route. Only forty-odd households reside there. Li Shouren, the village head, also practices traditional Chinese medicine. On the 14th of this month, he received 300 silver dollars. The following night, around 1:30 AM, thirty to forty bandits suddenly broke in and robbed his house. The robbers spoke with a Hubei accent and were armed with flashlights and guns. After robbing Li's house, they searched and robbed the homes of neighbors Li Yulin, Li Aying, and Li Ada, each losing about one to two hundred dollars. Li Shouren suffered the greatest loss, with over six hundred silver dollars, three gold rings, two pairs of gold bracelets, forty-odd pieces of clothing, two boxes of cotton cloth, five cotton quilts, a jar of salted fish, eight chickens, and a Western-style stove stolen. The search and robbery lasted for two hours before they fled fully loaded. Furthermore, in Xiejiaqiao Dongzhuanggang area, Jiuzhe District, there was a Ding Gen who died early, leaving behind a wife and daughter. However, their residence was in a desolate place with no neighbors. The night before last, five or six bandits suddenly arrived armed with pistols, broke down the door, restrained Mrs. Luo, and beat her with clubs. As a result, they were robbed of seven silver dollars, five pieces of foreign cloth clothing, and one pair of gold bracelets before leaving. Also, in Qixingqiao Niujiaweng, a place more than ten li outside Xiaodongmen, on the 16th, farmers reported banditry to the police, and six families, including Ji Shihe, Xu Genshou, Ji Jinsheng, Ji Jingen, Xu Genquan, and Ji Maomao, were robbed one after another. The loss of Ji Shihe's family was the greatest. Ji Jinsheng was seriously injured by the bandits. The villagers were intimidated and dared not report to the county government.

Kunshan 87

Expansion of Land Dispute in the Third District: The charted land in the former Lujia Hamlets of the Third District of this county amounts to about six to seven hundred mu. Since it was recovered from the hands of the village secretary in the second year of the Republic, it has been controlled by local despots in a series of transfers. No report has been made for eighteen years. Former District Head Yang Huai once submitted a resolution to the district affairs meeting and presented it to the county government's Department of Civil Affairs for approval to be reclaimed for the district. However, some township heads, secretly influenced and utilized, opposed it, leading to years of disputes. It is now heard that at the 21st District Head Meeting, it was decided that the charted land was of the same nature as the charted land currently managed by various districts. If measures are not taken to correct this, it will inevitably affect other districts, leading them to follow suit. This is a cause for concern for the future of local autonomy. It was decided that the ten district heads would jointly submit a report to the provincial authorities for review and approval.

Zhenjiang 88

Finance Department Urges Collection of Business Tax: Jiangsu Province is actively implementing the business tax. However, merchants are strongly arguing for a lower tax rate, making collection extremely difficult. Yesterday, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance issued a special order to the business tax collection bureaus of various counties, instructing them to collect and remit the taxes for April, May, and June within this month. The full text is recorded below: "It has been found that the Business Tax Law has been promulgated by the Legislative Yuan, and the business tax in this province should be levied as soon as possible without further delay. Now, I, the Director of this Department, based on the annual budget and considering the circumstances of each county, have tentatively determined the quota and submitted it to the 407th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee for discussion and approval, and the Provincial Government has ordered compliance, etc. In addition to distributing this, we hereby transcribe the original proposal and quota table to instruct the Director of the Bureau to comply with the prescribed quota, gradually investigate and squeeze, and earnestly collect the tax. All households that have previously reported inaccurately should also suspend the verification of books and records, conduct a detailed review, make accurate estimates, and submit a form for verification. Future collection procedures are stipulated to be collected quarterly. All collections for the first quarter from April to June should be collected and reported by the end of the month. Those who pay beyond the deadline will be dealt with in accordance with the penalty regulations, etc."

The Case of the Party Committee Falsely Accusing Comrades Opened Yesterday: Chen Shixian, Shi Shunyuan, Feng Guozhen, and others, former members of the Nanhui County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee, were investigated by the Provincial Party Headquarters and handed over to the Zhenjiang Court for handling due to privately engraving seals and falsely accusing comrades. Yesterday was the date for the court trial. It was heard that the court had issued more than ten subpoenas in advance, but only two witnesses, Chu Dongsheng and Zhang Xingsheng, reported yesterday. Chen Shixian and others were afraid of being punished and avoided appearing in court. They also planned to apply to the High Court for a transfer of jurisdiction in the hope of getting off scot-free.

The Murderer in the Jiang Buzhou Case Has Been Found: Jiang Buzhou, who lived in Baota Lane and ran a small restaurant, was shot and killed near the Dongyue Temple. The Sixth Public Security Bureau has successively arrested eight important suspects, including Li Shicai. After a brief interrogation, they were transferred to the Public Security Bureau. It is now learned that Jin Lunyuan, the section chief of the Judicial Section of the bureau, believed that the case involved murder with a gun and was of great importance. If he did not pay attention to the investigation, the truth would be difficult to determine. He conducted separate interrogations for days, using the testimony of one to corroborate the other. The suspects finally confessed the truth. The masterminds of the case were Zhang Zihuan and Li Shicai, and the perpetrator was Zhang Fengqi, who fired five shots that day. After the Public Security Bureau obtained the confession, it planned to send them to the Security Office for review today.

Provincial Government Borrows Money to Pay Salaries: The Provincial Government owed a large amount of salaries to the security teams of the Security Office and borrowed money from the Zhenjiang, Wuxi, and Wu County chambers of commerce to alleviate the urgent need. The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce has agreed to borrow 60,000 yuan, which will be advanced by the silver and money industry and guaranteed by various industries. The province will allow the business tax and grain transport tax of Zhenjiang as collateral.

Record of the Trial of Wang Shouyin for Neglect of Duty and Abuse of Power: Wang Shouyin, the former county police captain stationed in Baoyan Town, was reported for investigating and seizing opium in the house of Zhang Bao and privately releasing the suspect on bail without reporting the case, and was dismissed from his post and transferred to the court for investigation.

The criminal court filed a lawsuit, and it was heard that the case was publicly debated at 3:00 PM yesterday.

At that time, Judge Zhou of the Criminal Court presided over the trial in the Fourth Court and brought Wang Shouyin to court for interrogation. Witnesses Zhao Changkun and Yu Cuixing were also summoned to court for questioning. Yu was first summoned to court and testified that Wang was rarely at home and often away. Although he had heard about the opium case of Zhang Bao, he had not witnessed it. Wang and Zhao had never gambled together in people's homes. Once in March, they only watched a few cards and dispersed. Then Zhao Changkun testified that when investigating opium in Zhang Bao's house, he heard from outside the door that opium was found on the stove, but he did not witness it. He never gambled and did not know Cui Yuxing, etc.

Then Wang Shouyin was summoned to court and testified that the investigation and seizure of opium in Zhang's house was not his own decision, but that his subordinates had arrested the suspect, and he could not but question her. Later, because the suspect was seriously ill, she was released on bail. At that time, because the suppression of bandits and defense duties were tight, he did not report the case in time and only reported it after being transferred to the city. The procedure was wrong, and he requested a review. He himself did not gamble. The court rebuked him for not reporting to the court at that time, which inevitably made it appear that he was untruthful and incomplete. Wang stammered in response. Later, Prosecutor Zhu came to the court to make his arguments, and the court announced the end of the debate. Wang then requested bail, and Judge Zhong instructed that the case had been concluded and there was no need for bail. He could wait for the judgment and then review it. Then he announced that the case would be sentenced at 2:00 PM on the 23rd of this month. Wang was still returned to custody, and Zhao was released on his original bail.

Yu was ordered to return and leave the court.

He was informed that he should report to the post office on June 20th to inspect various postal items and was instructed to take his work seriously and not to be negligent.

Urging Repayment of Rice Borer Eradication Loan: In Jiaxing during the 13th year of the Republic, the rice borer infestation was severe, and there were insufficient funds for eradication. The former county council resolved that the former magistrate, Li Shouci, should forward a request for a provincial loan of 10,000 yuan for use, and the 10% reduction in the provincial tax under the compensation fund was changed to the county's rice borer eradication expenses to be collected and repaid. The province approved the plan. However, the funds have not yet been returned to the provincial treasury. The Department of Finance investigated and found that Jiaxing County has insect control funds, in addition to the 10% rice borer eradication bond fund, and has been collecting two dimes of silver for insect control.

It has been several years and it is expected that the loan can be repaid. Yesterday, the county was ordered to strictly urge the Rice Borer Eradication Association to promptly allocate and repay the aforementioned reserve funds to the treasury, in order to value public funds.

China Science Society 101

Announces Selection of Archeology Award Recipient ▲ Winner: Pei Wenzhong – Annual Meeting Changed to Zhenjiang: The China Science Society established the Archeology Award starting in the 19th year, with an annual gold medal and a cash prize of 100 yuan. The award committee recommends one person with the best archeological research results in the country to the board of directors for the award. The award for the 19th year has been agreed upon by the committee members Ding Wenjiang, Weng Wenhao, and Zhang Zhao to be given to Pei Wenzhong. The 95th board meeting of the society has approved this. Mr. Pei's work achievements are published as follows: Pei Wenzhong joined the Zhoukoudian fossil collection organized by the Geological Survey in the 17th year of the Republic. In the 18th year, Mr. Pei independently took charge of this excavation work, continuing until the summer of the 19th year. During this work period, Mr. Pei discovered many valuable fossils. Now, Bu Dasheng, Yang Zhongjian, and Mr. Pei are separately studying various fossils. What is particularly praised by the world is the Peking Man fossil.

In addition to fragmented teeth, a fairly complete Peking Man skull was discovered on December 2, 18. In July of the 19th year, another Peking Man skull collected in October of the 18th year was found while sorting materials. This skull is not only more complete than the Java Man, but also an important material for studying the bones of early humans. At the same time, a large number of other animal fossils were completely preserved, which confirmed that they lived at the same time as Peking Man. Unlike the Java fossils, which were from the alluvial era, the study of these animal fossils can determine the geological age more accurately than that of any other hominid fossil found elsewhere. Mr. Pei also participated in the study of this paleontology. Some of it can be published now. Mr. Pei's rare discoveries, large-scale excavation work, and existing research work have been recognized by other specialists and praised by the world's academic community. All should receive considerable encouragement from the Chinese academic community.

In addition, the society's annual meeting this year was originally scheduled to be held at Northeastern University in Shenyang. It was reported in this newspaper. Recently, due to inconvenient preparations, the society's board of directors decided to change the location to Zhenjiang. The meeting will be held from August 22nd to 26th. The list of members of the annual meeting preparation committee has also been reorganized as follows: Wu Zhihui (Chairman), Mao Tangchen, Zheng Zaicen, Yang Yunzhong,

(Above are standing committee members) Sun Kuibo, Chen Mengzhao, Liu Mou, Yu Qingtang, Zhou Xingbei. This Local

Shanghai Municipality Inquires About How to Connect Large, Medium, and Small School Admissions: The Ministry of Education previously received a report from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education stating that the city's private secondary schools mostly adopt a dual-track system for student admission, with both spring and autumn semester classes. However, the city's private universities only have autumn semester classes, making it difficult for spring graduates to find immediate opportunities for further education. It is proposed that the bureau transfer the matter to the universities, devising ways to increase the convenience for spring graduates of Shanghai's secondary schools to enter universities. The Ministry has examined the university regulations issued by the Ministry and the revision of Article 14 of Chapter 4 of the specialized school regulations, stipulating that entrance examinations should be held at the beginning of each academic year. Therefore, students entering specialized schools and above should begin in the fall. Also, the provisional regulations for primary and secondary schools promulgated by the former University Council do not explicitly stipulate the beginning of the academic year, but the beginning of the academic year and the regulations of the school calendar all start in the fall. It is an exception for schools to start in the spring. However, it is a long-standing habit among the people in various places to send their young children to primary school in early spring. Therefore, primary schools have a dual-track system of starting in spring and autumn, which is also followed by private secondary schools, which are motivated to enroll more students. Therefore, there is no problem in connecting the timing of graduating from primary school and entering secondary school, 102

However, the timing of graduating from secondary school and entering specialized schools and above cannot be connected due to regulations, resulting in difficulties. Now, according to the requests of the private secondary schools, it seems that it is necessary to connect the timing of admission to large, medium, and small schools in the future. However, the bureau did not dare to make a decision on its own, whether to follow the people's habits and have universities add spring semester classes, or to strictly order primary and secondary schools to restrict the enrollment of spring semester students, and submitted a report for review. The Ministry of Education instructed that the spring semester classes in primary and secondary schools are intended to add classes, expand enrollment, and save repeating time for repeaters, not specifically to seek convenience for those seeking further education. The bureau believes that because specialized schools and above mostly start in the fall, spring graduates of secondary schools have difficulty entering school and proposes to restrict primary and secondary schools from enrolling spring semester students. This is difficult to approve. As for universities, if they are economically well-off, they can add spring semester classes, but there is no need to issue a general order for uniform implementation. Let it be known.

Municipal Party Department 103

Publishes Guidelines for Party Teacher Registration: Since the Training Department of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department began holding reviews and registrations for Party ideology teachers and training directors on the 10th of this month, there have been many inquiries about review and registration procedures from current and aspiring Party ideology teachers and training directors who have visited the department. It is heard that the review and registration period is three months, ending on September 10th. The "Guidelines for Requesting Review and Registration as a Party Ideology Teacher" formulated by the department are published below for public viewing.

▲ Guidelines for Requesting Review and Registration as a Party Ideology Teacher (1) Personnel who must request review: those who are currently or aspire to be Party ideology teachers and training directors but have not been examined; (2) Personnel who must request registration: 1. Party ideology teachers who have passed the examination; 2. Those who have served as members of the Party ideology teacher examination committee; 3. Those who have served as Party ideology teachers for more than two years; (3) Methods for determining qualifications: 1. Those who have served or are currently serving in positions above the level of director in provincial and municipal party departments for two years or more, or members of county and city party departments who have studied at secondary schools and have researched party ideology, may request to be given qualifications to serve as Party ideology teachers in secondary schools; 2. Those who have served or are currently serving in positions above the level of staff member in provincial party departments for two years or more, and have graduated from elementary school, may request to be given qualifications to serve as Party ideology teachers in elementary schools; 3. Party members who have graduated from party affairs schools with qualifications equivalent to those of teachers in schools at each level; 4. Probationary party members who have served in education for more than three years and have qualifications equivalent to those of schools at each level; 5. The determination of qualifications for requesting registration shall remain the same; (4) Procedures for requesting review or registration: 1. Fill out and submit the review form (i.e., application form and resume), and attach one copy of the party membership card; 2. Attach three 2-inch half-length photos; 4. Attach the graduation certificate, service certificate, and all supporting documents (those requesting registration may exchange them for the examination certificate); (5) Only one form needs to be filled out, but it must be detailed and clear, and omissions and carelessness are not allowed, and the form must be stamped; (6) All academic qualifications and experiences must be accompanied by supporting documents, otherwise the information filled out will not be counted. However, the above documents can be attached to the degree that is suitable for the qualifications requested for review,

There is no need to list and attach too many; (7) When submitting the review form, all required procedures and services must be fully prepared to facilitate the review; (8) The order of review by the committee will be based on the order in which the forms are submitted and the completeness of the procedures; after the review is completed, if it is deemed appropriate, a certificate will be issued and announced in the newspaper, the same applies to those requesting registration; (9) The review and registration period is set for three months, ending on September 10; (10) To request a review form (i.e., application form and resume) and review regulations by mail, enclose a one-cent postage stamp; empty letters will not be replied to.

City Bureau of Education 104

Distribution of Ten Drops of Water to Subordinate Rural Institutions The City Bureau of Education approved the Health Bureau's letter requesting the distribution of 500 bottles of Ten Drops Water medicine, stating that regardless of the type of Ten Drops Water, it can only be used as a temporary medicine for heatstroke and has no effect on preventing or treating severe illnesses such as cholera. For cholera prevention, it is still necessary to get cholera vaccinations and pay attention to food hygiene, etc. Since schools in the Shanghai South and Zhabei districts can easily purchase such medicine, the Bureau of Education distributed this medicine to subordinate rural schools and public education centers for their use. Schools and centers can pick them up at any time.

Ministry of Education Organizes Committee to Set Standards for Primary and Secondary School Curricula and Equipment The Elementary School Group Met Yesterday - The Secondary School Group Will Meet Today - Party Principles Not Specifically Taught in Junior Elementary School; Content Integrated Into Various Subjects Health Subject Established, First Article of General Objectives of Early Childhood Education Revised The Ministry of Education's temporary standards for primary and secondary school curricula will expire after one year of experimentation. The Ministry of Education has reorganized the original drafting committee into the "Committee for Compiling Standards for Primary and Secondary School Curricula and Equipment" and appointed additional members to revise the curriculum standards based on the opinions gathered from various experiments, in order to formally announce and implement them. For the convenience of discussion, the committee divided all members into primary and secondary school groups. Yesterday (the 18th), starting at 8:30 AM, the primary school group met at the Ministry of Education to discuss primary school standards. The secondary school group will meet today and tomorrow (the 19th and 20th). The Ministry of Education sent each member a copy of the opinions on the curriculum standards from various parties and the Ministry of Education's questions about the curriculum standards in advance, requesting that they study the details and bring their opinions to Beijing. Members who could not attend in person were asked to send their opinions to the Ministry in advance for discussion. The list of members appointed by the Ministry of Education for the primary and secondary school groups and the details of yesterday's meeting are recorded separately below: 114

▲ Details of the Primary School Group Meeting Nanjing, 18th The Ministry of Education Committee for Compiling Standards for Primary and Secondary School Curriculum Equipment Elementary School Group meeting, held at the Ministry of Education Conference Hall starting at 9:00 AM on the 18th until adjournment at 5:00 PM, attended by Committee Shen Baiying, et al. Chairman Gu Shusen. Items discussed

A. Ministry of Education's Views on Elementary School Curriculum Standards, Resolutions, 1. The Citizenship curriculum for junior elementary school is incorporated into the social studies curriculum and is not set up as a separate subject. 2. Party Principles not specifically set up for junior elementary school; the teaching materials are contained in each subject.

3. The two teaching materials, public health and personal hygiene, are combined into one and combined with physical education to form a health subject, divided into two categories: hygiene and physical education.

4. The question of social studies teaching materials is submitted to the Subject Review Committee for discussion, but the standard of modification should be more concrete than the original one. 5. In the explanation of work subjects, the explanation of each operation should be explained, and the minimum should be modified and submitted to the subject review committee for discussion, and the commercial item should retain the names and the content of the operation should be submitted to the subject review committee for revision. 6. Resolution to add a total goal, nominate a committee to draft based on the principle of the Three People's Principles, and draft teaching rules. 7. Whether to select at least a limited number of words, the question should be submitted to the Chinese Language Subject Review Committee for discussion.

8. The total time for each subject should be redistributed after the time for each subject is determined.

B. Each committee member's temporary opinions on the complete revision, resolved, 1. The question of subject consolidation should be discussed together by the members drafting the teaching rules during the drafting process. 2. The time for extracurricular activities should be specified when the general explanation is revised. 3. When the Subject Review Committee meets,

pay attention to the minimum level of each subject, 4. Regarding the order of subjects, the health interest should be listed under the party principles, and the remaining subjects should still be arranged in order.

C. Opinions of each committee member on the revision of each subject, resolution, 1. The first article of the general objective of early childhood education is changed to "Enhance the health and due happiness and happiness of young children", nominate members of each subject review committee, 1. Health Early Childhood Education Group members: Chen Heqin, Ma Ketan, Hu Shuyi, Shen Leiyu, 2. Chinese Language Arithmetic Group Shi Renyun, Shen Baiying, Zhu Wenshu, Lin Duanfu, 3. 4. Work Art Music Group Wu Yanin Jiang Zhongcen Bo Tianhan

D. The date of the next meeting will be at 10:00 AM on the 20th to continue the second general meeting, the secondary school group will meet today and tomorrow to discuss

▲ Ministry of Education's Opinion on Revising the Elementary School Curriculum Temporary Standards 1. Regarding the secondary school curriculum, (1) Whether to add a civic science subject in high schools or add the words "and civic science subject" under "Party Principles", (2) Whether the level of each subject in high school should be appropriately lowered, focusing on basic practice, (3) Whether the required subjects in high school should be appropriately reduced and the number of elective subjects should be increased, so as to leave room for local activities, (4) Whether the elective subjects in high school should be divided into liberal arts, science, vocational and other groups, so that those who choose to study can specialize in similar subjects, (5) There is a lot of repetition of teaching materials in high and junior high schools, and it is too uneconomical for students preparing to enter school. Should junior high schools be divided into two parts, one specializing in those preparing to enter school, and its curriculum should be changed to a direct-entry type, and one specializing in those not entering school, which should be extended by one year and application subjects such as vocational courses should be added? 2. Regarding the primary school curriculum, (1) The Central Training Department advocates that Party Principles should not be specifically set up in junior elementary schools, and that the teaching materials should be incorporated into each subject. Which subject is the most suitable for incorporating Party Principles teaching materials among the existing subjects? What kind of Party Principles teaching materials should be incorporated into which subject? (2) Should citizenship education be specifically set up in elementary schools, or should it be merged into social studies education? Should civil public education materials be included in high elementary school Party Principles education? Should civic teaching materials be merged into social studies education? (3) Sanitation teaching materials are divided into two. Some people advocate that it is better to merge it into natural science. How should these claims be resolved? (4) Is the basic knowledge of history and geography lacking in the social studies teaching materials for senior grades? (5) It is said that the content of work science is complicated and should be reorganized, or it is said that it does not need to be reorganized.

How should the decision be made? How should the word "work" be changed to match the subject operation? (6) Should the goals and teaching methods of each subject be repeated? Should "General Goals" and "Teaching Rules" be proposed and added after the explanation?

A Thought 115

— Holding Buddha

▲ Beauties are endowed with the essence of heaven and earth, so it is not easy to find them. Just like a masterpiece of writing, it may not come from the hand of someone with a great reputation. Therefore, in a place with beautiful mountains and clear waters, there may be extraordinary beauties that are unmatched in the city.

▲ Planting famous flowers in cow dung is more aesthetically offensive than burning a zither and cooking a crane.

▲ Mirrors are the confidantes of beauties, lamps are their good companions, and flowers are their reflections.

▲ Women who engage in carnal life on the sea often support their parents and raise their younger siblings. The act is shameful, but the intention is pitiful. Those who are seven feet tall and cannot fulfill their filial duties should be ashamed to die.

▲ Prostitutes may not want to be prostitutes. The reason why they eventually fall and cannot extricate themselves is often the encirclement of the procuress. The same is true for military men who are surrounded by politicians.

▲ The magic power of the eyes to colors and the ears to sounds is ultimately inferior to "touch". This is because the eyes and ears still belong to the six senses, while touch goes directly into the eight consciousness fields. The Romance of the Western Chamber says, "A little numbness comes on." Is this the reason?

▲ Westerners wrote a novel called "The World Cannibal Club", which roughly says that a train was trapped in the ice and snow of Siberia. When the food was exhausted, cannibalism was practiced. Later, someone made an experiential statement, saying, "Men's meat is as hard as iron, and women's meat is as soft as cotton." In fact, men's and women's meat are equally soft and hard. This is because even in this desperate situation, a little lust has not been extinguished.

▲ It is easier for women to become famous than men. The same is true for monks.

A Record of the Secret Tribunal 116

— Jie Fei

During the thirteenth century, there were more than three hundred small states standing along the Rhine River in Germany. Politics were neglected and laws differed. Murder and robbery were seen everywhere at any time. However, the Germans were inherently strong and chivalrous, so they secretly organized secret tribunals, Vehm or Fehm, as a means of self-defense. It became popular throughout Germany for a time. Two centuries later, the Holy Roman Emperor, the seven electors, and the archbishops once took it as an honor to兼get security.

The origin of the secret tribunal in Europe is not recorded in Western history. It flourished in the thirteenth century. It first issued a warrant to the offender who could not be dealt with by the law, ordering him to be tried at a certain place on a certain day. The conviction was determined by one trial. It was either capital punishment or freedom. There were only these two ways. If the person did not arrive after receiving the warrant, the secret tribunal sent an officer to arrest him. One out of a hundred could escape. If three people in the court encountered a murderer, they should put the murderer to death without waiting for the court's judgment. The four letters S·S·G·G were written on the wood. People knew that it was done by the people in the secret tribunal and dared not investigate.

In the beginning, it eliminated violence and maintained peace, forced the strong to restrain themselves, and the social order was quite sufficient to maintain for a while. Later, it was used to retaliate for grudges, and the abuse was excessive, and its style declined.

One Day on Dragon Pond Mountain 117

— Rui Hongchu

I have long heard that the scenery of Longtan Mountain in Liyang is extraordinary. It is even better than the West Lake in Hangzhou. A few days ago, I made an appointment with my friends Liu Youxian and Jin Binglan, as well as my wife and daughter, and five or six other people to take a boat to visit. The mountain is located in the south of Liyang City, more than forty miles away from the city, passing through Daibu Town. From the town upwards, the road is surrounded by pine and bamboo, the stream flows under your feet, mountain flowers are scattered, and wild birds compete to fly, making people feel like they are entering a paradise. After advancing a few more miles, there are overlapping mountains, and streams of water fly from the stones. Only the sound of water can be heard. We sat on the stones for a while, and suddenly saw a woodcutter carrying firewood on his shoulders from the green shade. We immediately asked him what ancient sites were on Longtan Mountain. The woodcutter replied, "A few miles away is the Longtan Temple newly built by Zen Master Kangdian. There is also the place where Immortal He practiced alchemy, the Alchemy Well, the Alchemy Stove, and the place where the great Confucian scholar Chen Bianruo of the late Ming Dynasty lived in seclusion. There are cliffs for several miles, and waterfalls cascade down. Further into the south of Longshan Mountain, hundreds of acres of plum blossoms are in full bloom. There is a small village in the middle where you can ask for tea to quench your thirst. Further up for about a mile, there is a Fairy Stone Cave, which can be entered with a candle." After the woodcutter finished speaking, he carried his firewood and left. We passed through a bamboo path and over a small stream, and saw the temple towering on the mountainside. We quickly went straight up along the small path among the pines and passed another stream to reach Longtan Temple. Entering the temple, we saw the solemn Buddha statues and the simple furnishings, but we did not see a monk in the temple for a long time. Only in the deep valley south of the temple, there was an old man, over sixty years old, wearing a bamboo hat and straw shoes, carrying a bamboo stick in his hand, leaning on the right side of the peach blossom stone dock, his eyes shining, as if a dharma light was radiating outward. We turned around the stone wall, stepped forward to salute, and asked if there was a great monk in the temple. The old man replied, "Where did the great laymen come from? I am the monk Kangdian." He then invited us into the temple, drew water from Longtan Spring, and cooked wild mountain tea, which tasted fragrant and sweet. Then he served us with coarse rice, wild vegetables, and vegetable roots. After we had eaten our fill, Kangdian laughed and said, "If you can put such coarse rice and vegetable roots into your belly, you are not lacking in good roots." I heard that Kangdian was familiar with Mr. Shi Liangcai and Mr. Wang Yiting in Shanghai, and he liked to chant and was good at calligraphy. The plaque of the Maitreya Pavilion in Lingyin Temple in Hangzhou was written by him. I asked for a couplet, which said, "Pond fish know the nature of water, wild birds are pleased with the fragrance of flowers." The brushwork is vigorous and worthy of treasure. Kangdian recently traveled between Six Bridges and Three Tianzhu Temples and moored his boat by the lake of Jingci Temple. He has a poem that says: "Deep in the lotus flowers, I drink the fragrance. It doesn't hurt to recite Amitabha. The breeze rolls up the ripples without vulgarity. The red dust is far away from the land of clouds and water." He also inscribed a poem on the stone railing of the Great Buddha Temple, saying: "Once again a bell rings in the old trees. The six bridges roll the setting sun red. Enthusiastically purify the land beyond the mundane. Cold-faced West Lake laughs at the drunken old man." After we finished our tour, Kangdian happily saw us off for several miles. His enthusiasm was touching. We then arrived at a small village and rested at a farmer's house. The old farmer offered fragrant tea as a treat. I asked about Kangdian's background. The old farmer replied, "Kangdian was a Hanlin scholar in the Qing Dynasty. He once served as a military commander and was also the editor of the Hubei Qunbao. Because of the constant turmoil in the country in recent years, he was disheartened and became a monk to live in seclusion here." The next day, we returned to Shanghai and recorded it to leave a mark.

A Few Drops 118

— (Cuckoo)

Watching Xun Huisheng's performance of the literary meeting is like Yun Nantian setting the colors of peach blossoms in the daytime. The emotions are enchanting, but the hairpin phoenix drama is like a sprig of autumn begonia. It is the blood in the eyes of a thoughtful woman.

Notes on Reading Paintings in the Art Garden 119

— Too Thin Student

My friends Ma Wanli, Wu Ziding, and Zhao Banbo have been immersed in poetry, books, and paintings day and night. From the 13th, they jointly held a painting exhibition for three days at the Ningbo Fellow Association on Tibet Road. I went there with He Tianjian and was already intoxicated in the Wushuang Studio, so I drove to visit again. I felt that the walls were full of exquisite paintings and colorful clouds were fluttering. The air of worldliness was washed away from there.

Wanli loved art since he was a child. His family was rich in collections, and he spent all day flipping through them, so he gained a unique understanding. Painting is a reflection of character. With Wanli's pure talent and transcendence, his paintings are light, distant, precipitous, and free from worldliness. He imitated Tianchi Fudao in his paintings, but they are sweet and rich. His painting of morning glories is a unique expression of spirituality. The colors are rich and moist, and the interests are full and round. Tianjian wrote a poem while drunk, saying: "The painted morning glories are not fragrant. Pan Lang wants to break his nine-turned intestines. The Weaver Girl's cloud brocade is left in vain. How can it be helped that the days and months in the world are long?" It is said that Wanli recently wrote an elegy for his deceased wife. This painting and this poem express deep feelings. It is said that Wanli's wife, Ms. Tang Meiqian, was also good at art. Now she has gone to the jade palace, leaving only long sighs. Ziding was a student in Xiuning and served as an official in all directions. He was skilled in meticulous figure painting, especially similar to Gai Qixiang. In his later years, he regained the charm of Wen Zhengming and Tang Yin and was praised by the art world. Among the paintings on display, the two paintings "When the Autumn Wind is Clear and the Geese Come" and "Sitting Late in the Maple Forest" were the most outstanding. As for Mr. Zhao Banbo, it is a good story in the art world that he, an old man in his seventies, is fond of this and never tires of it. Banbo began to learn painting after the age of fifty. The gnarled roots and intertwined branches have the flavor of Bada Shanren. Recently, he has also participated in the divine posture of Bai Yang and Xin Luo. The bone charm of Dong Xin's jade table makes it feel more elegant and unrestrained. However, he is clumsy in being an official and does not live in a rich place. He relies on painting to comfort himself. It is said that Banbo retired to painting with the talent of a law-abiding official. His paintings are rich in poetic meaning, and the pen and paintings are full of flavor. (Thanks for the reward)

Research on Famine Relief Foods (Part 1) 121

— Tianxu Wosheng

A letter from Mr. Xiang Shanxing states that the various famine relief methods recorded in the newly compiled "Verified Formulas" are quite simple and easy to implement. However, he has doubts about whether they are beneficial or harmless to human physiology. Xu has reviewed the first formula, which consists of three sheng of glutinous rice and three sheng of sesame seeds. Each is washed clean with water and stir-fried over low heat. First, grind the glutinous rice into flour, then add the sesame seeds and grind them together into a powder. Then, use three jin of red dates, boil them until soft, remove the skin and pits, and mash them into a paste. Mix the paste with the powder and form into pills, each weighing five qian. Eat one pill daily, chased down with boiling water, to alleviate hunger. If glutinous rice and red dates are unavailable, japonica rice and black dates can be used instead. This formula is essentially the "er su" crisps made in the Hangzhou nunneries, but instead of being made into pills, they are made into bite-sized crisps. They are extremely fragrant and delicious and require chewing. Eating only two such crisps can quell hunger for four hours, with each crisp weighing approximately four qian. However, eating too many can cause chest tightness and discomfort, so it is best to chew them slowly, accompanied by tea. My family has often made this as food and it is nothing new. According to human physiology and hygiene, the daily nutritional requirements for an average laborer are 130 to 150 grams of protein, 84 grams of fat, 404 grams of starch, 2800 grams of water, and 30 grams of salt. Protein is vitamin A, a nitrogenous substance. One jin of ordinary rice contains only 36 grams of protein, while one jin of glutinous rice contains 84 grams. One jin of sesame seeds contains more than 123 grams. Therefore, one sheng of sesame seeds is equivalent to three and a half sheng of ordinary rice, and one sheng of glutinous rice is equivalent to two and a half sheng of ordinary rice. The methods of the ancients are indeed in line with reason and chemistry. Their ability to investigate things and pursue principles has reached its peak, but it is simply not noticed through familiarity. A comparison table is listed below, with the content of 600 grams (16 taels) as the standard:

Ingredient　Protein　Fat　Water　Carbohydrate　Notes

Rice　36 grams　12　444

Wheat　60　12　384　One sheng equals 1.7 sheng of rice

Glutinous Rice　84　39.6　456　One sheng equals 2.33 sheng of rice

Sesame　123.3　309.4　75.6　One sheng equals 3.5 sheng of rice

As can be seen from the above, glutinous rice and sesame seeds are rich in protein and can achieve more with less. However, their fat content is excessive, and gastric juices cannot fully digest them, so they should be stir-fried to evaporate the oil. The addition of jujube paste is simply to make them easy to knead and mix. Dates are beneficial for the spleen and stomach, as detailed in the "Compendium of Materia Medica." Therefore, this first formula is definitely usable.

The second formula states: take equal parts of chestnuts, red dates, and walnuts, all skinned, and persimmon cakes, with the stems removed. Steam for one to two hours, take them out, and mash them extremely finely in a stone mortar. Press into thick cakes, which are prepared and dried in winter for storage. One cake can last three to four days without hunger, and taking another cake after three to four days can last even longer. It is said to nourish the kidneys, strengthen the spleen, moisten the lungs, and clear the liver, but it must be chewed carefully.

Three Eras (10) 122

— Zhang Henshui

However, the policemen's guns were not usually aimed at the common people. Shooting was always the prerogative of the boss. So, the policemen, hearing the soldiers cursing, usually tolerated it, pretending they didn't hear it, and just tried their best to pull the fighting rickshaw pullers apart and take them to the district office. Zhang Xiaosan said, "Hey, patrolmen, get out of the way! Don't interfere with the rickshaw pullers. Let them fight their own battles. What's it to you?" The policemen, seeing him shouting it out loud, could no longer pretend to be deaf. They said, "We're maintaining order. We can't let them fight in the street. We're doing our duty. What's it to you?" Zhang Xiaosan said, "We'll beat you bastards! Let you see that being a 'rubber hose squad' member is nothing. There are seven or eight former 'rubber hose squad' members in this row of soldiers!" They shouted in unison, "Beat them!" And they swarmed forward, punching and kicking the three policemen, aiming everywhere. Zhang Xiaosan was especially skilled at fighting. He took off his belt and, holding one end, used it like a whip, lashing out wildly. The onlookers retreated far away, worried for the policemen. Some hooligans and wild children, however, clapped and cheered. The three policemen initially wanted to fight back, planning to grab one or two of the soldiers. But then the whole row of soldiers mobilized, and the three policemen had no choice but to turn and run, leaving two police caps behind. Zhang Xiaosan, panting, fastened his belt. He picked up a police baton and a police cap from the ground and held the baton, with the cap on top, high above his head, laughing loudly. Another soldier snatched it and threw it on the ground, laughing, "Stop it! The platoon leader is scolding us." Zhang Xiaosan puffed out his chest, tossed his head, and said, "My time in the army wasn't wasted. I finally got some satisfaction today!" He took off his military cap, wiped the sweat from his forehead with his hand, and then slammed the military cap onto his head, with the visor pointing upwards, exposing a large part of his forehead, and swaggered back to the ranks. This incident had no impact. Only the next day, a piece of social news in the newspaper reported that some people wearing grey cloth short coats had a minor conflict with the police at the entrance of the Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce. The situation was quickly resolved. Not only was the army unit not mentioned, but even the word "soldier" was omitted. So, in addition to going to the garden for nothing and riding the tram for nothing, they now had the added benefit of beating the police for nothing.

Discount Prices End Low 125

▲Market Overview: The financial world typically experiences a downturn during the summer months. This year, due to poor cocoon yields, foreign sales have been significantly hindered, and silver has fewer applications, resulting in a decline in silver prices. Additionally, the summer harvest in the countryside is not very plentiful, which is suppressing commercial activity. Since finance is the core of all industries, each industry naturally experiences a decline as well. Therefore, current business conditions are weakened along with the market.

▲Discounted Prices: (Silver Dollars) The discount price in the early market remained at 7 qian, 2 fen, 5 li, 6 hao, 2 hu, 5 si, the same as the previous afternoon. However, the afternoon market was slightly better by 3 hao, 7 hu, 5 si, at 7 qian, 2 fen, 6 li. The overall trend was mostly downward, ultimately remaining low. (Silver Futures) Both the early and afternoon markets were at 6 fen, with a premium of 4 to 5 fen, slightly lower than the previous day.

▲Subsidiary Coin Market: Jiangnan small silver coins remained unchanged in both the early and afternoon markets, at 6 qian, 4 fen, 7 li, and trading was inactive. Guangdong small silver coins were at 6 qian, 4 fen, 5 li, 5 hao in the early market and 6 qian, 4 fen, 4 li, 5 hao in the afternoon market, a difference of one li. Transactions occurred, with 110,000 jiao in the early market and 35,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Copper coins decreased by another 1,500 wen, totaling 377,500 wen. Over 30,000 strings were traded.

▲Silver Dollar Inflow and Outflow: (Silver) Bank deposits were moderate yesterday. Chinese banks deposited over 2.8 million in banknotes. Foreign banks deposited over 1.89 million in banknotes, over 1 million in special deposits, and over 10.67 million in various goods, foreign exchange, taxes, and miscellaneous deposits. 500,000 entered the warehouse, and 300,000 exited the warehouse. Japanese banks deposited over 4.8 million in various deposits, 600,000 entered the warehouse, and money houses deposited over 48.8 million in banknotes, over 4.2 million in premium deposits, over 1.1 million in remittances, and tens of thousands in cash. (Silver Dollars) Over 1.77 million in remittances were made in the early market and over 990,000 in the afternoon market. 65,000 in banknotes were made in the early market and 30,000 in the afternoon market. 172,000 in external banknotes were made in the early market and 85,000 in the afternoon market. Bank trading amounted to 720,000 in interbank transactions in the early market and 600,000 in interbank transactions in the afternoon market. Bank accounts received and released over 1.4 million in deposits, and over 1.78 million in banknotes were recovered and issued. Money houses deposited over 5.9 million in silver dollar banknotes, over 2.5 million in silver dollar premium deposits, over 1.5 million in silver dollar loans, and over 900,000 in small money house transactions.

Securities: Bond Prices Fall Sharply 126

▲1920 Customs Bond Drops by Over 1.5 Yuan　　▲Remaining Bonds Also Weak; Transactions Reach Over 19 Million: Yesterday, the bond market in Shanghai saw limited spot trading in the Disbandment Bond, while other bonds saw no trading. The futures market remained active. Trading in July contracts increased compared to previous days. The changes in each bond showed a significant decline as the market opened, falling by around one yuan, but after the initial drop, supply and demand stabilized. After this point prices remained range bound. Consequently, closing prices were much lower compared to the previous day, including 1920 Customs Bond, July and June, and 196 July and June each down 1.7 yuan, Disbandment and Troop Reduction, 20 and Customs bonds also down around one yuan. The 1996 saw still minor fluctuations. Total spot transactions of only one thousand dollars, and futures trading reached over 12 million in the morning and 7 million in the afternoon, amounting to 19.4 million. The 20 customs bond accounted for over 7.4 million yuan.

Yarn & Cotton: Market Sees Increase in Bearish Sentiment 127

▲Cotton Yarn Market to Close for One Day on the 20th

The yarn market opened lower in the morning but rose in the afternoon, with the market remaining tense. The condition of foreign cotton yarn was stable, and actual sales were relatively brisk. Tianjin merchants remained active in making offers, but there was a lack of available stock, causing the prices of 16 and 20 count yarns to be exceptionally tight. The market was very firm. Business for 10 count coarse yarn was especially lacking. Japanese merchants continued to offer sales in distant months. A portion of large short sellers closed out their positions in large quantities and flipped to long positions, resulting in unusually dry trading. As a result, the market has become increasingly tight.

▲Speculators Cover Shorts: Pre-market opening at the exchange showed that with U.S. cotton being flat and actual sales stagnant, the market was somewhat loose, with prices falling by 6, 7, 8, and 9 qian. After the market closed in the afternoon, prices surged by 7 qian to 1.45 taels due to short covering in a market without sufficient volume. Total trading was estimated at 60,000 bales. Shenxin sold 1,350 bales, Rongxing sold 1,800 bales, Shenchang sold 1,700 bales, Yongfeng sold 5,050 bales, Senkang sold 1,850 bales, Yuantai sold 1,600 bales, and Xincheng sold 1,050 bales. Gengfeng sold 2,250 bales. Tianlong bought 3,050 bales, Taixing bought 1,250 bales, Yiyu bought 3,450 bales, Gengfeng bought 2,100 bales, and Yichang bought 2,300 bales. The closing prices are recorded below.

Reasons for the Sudden Rise in Cotton Prices 128

▲Major Players Shift from Short to Long Positions… 30,000 to 40,000 Bales in Two Days Cotton market trends are firming. Although overseas cotton markets and gold prices are mediocre, the local market has seen a general shift from short to long positions by major players due to rising yarn prices. In the past two days, contract volumes have reached approximately 30,000 to 40,000 bales, resulting in a remarkably tight supply. Consequently, market prices have soared.

▲Hankow Standard Cotton Closes with Significant Gains The Exchange's Hankow Standard cotton market was flat in the morning, with prices falling by 1.5 to 2 cents. The market remained flat after the afternoon opening, but prices suddenly rebounded by 3 to 5 cents at the 3:00 PM closing. Total transaction volume reached 70,700 bales. Sales included 3,200 bales from Mei Kee, 1,700 bales from Rong Xing, 2,700 bales from Geng Feng, and 1,000 bales from Shen Kee. Purchases included 7,000 bales from Tian Long, 1,400 bales from Chang Feng, 1,900 bales from Yi Chang, and 1,800 bales from Yu Da. The closing prices for Hankow Standard cotton are recorded below: Hankow Standard Closing Prices (Rise/Fall) Account Balance August: 40.30 (+.25) 53,600 bales June: 39.95 (+.20) 77,500 bales October: 38.40 201,639 bales July: 40.35 (+.35) 52,100 bales November: 38.00 118,800 bales

▲No Spot Market Transactions Reported No transactions in spot cotton have been reported. Sources include 300 bales of "Wooden Frame" cotton and 220 bales of "Through" cotton, it is said.

Simultaneous Decline in U.S. Cotton and Sanpin (Osaka Three Commodities) 129

▲U.S. Cotton Sees Southern Selling Yesterday, U.S. cotton initially firmed due to buying by industry participants, but later weakened due to selling from the South and favorable weather conditions. Futures fell by 7 to 9 points, while spot prices fell by 5 points. U.K. cotton futures rose by 10 to 11 points, with spot prices up by 11 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices rose by 15 points. Indian cotton weakened due to selling by European exporters and profit-taking by bullish investors, closing quiet but stable. Prices for Pingguo'er were unchanged, Aomula rose by 1 rupee, and Bairuoxi fell by 1 rupee. Silk and Tea: European and American Silk Sales Still Difficult 130

In the European and American markets, Japanese silk merchants are competitively selling new crop silk, causing prices to weaken. As a result, Chinese and Italian silk merchants are not quoting high prices. Chinese merchants, having substantial holdings, are only slightly adjusting prices in response to telegrams, making it difficult to boost sales. Yesterday, only Jardine Matheson and others imported 30 bales of Shanghai white filature silk, while Qianli and others imported 70 bales of white dried silk. Prices remained stable, it is said.

New Danyang Native Silk Enters the Market 131

▲Poor Silk Quality… Fine Silk at 46 Yuan, Thick Silk at 40 Yuan This year's spring silkworm cocoons in various towns and villages of Danyang were exceptionally scarce due to unfavorable weather conditions, and the cocoons were also of poor quality. Cocoon merchants refused to accept inferior cocoons, so villagers are reeling their own native silk and bringing it to market for sale. Silk merchants in the city have officially opened for business. Because the silk color is dark and of secondary quality, prices are not high. High-quality fine silk is only fetching 46 yuan per 100 taels, while thick silk is fetching 40 yuan. Few merchants are buying, it is said.

Qimen Zi Tea Prices Surge by 40-50 Yuan 132

This year's Qimen black tea, due to the dedicated improvements by various tea estates,

emphasizes the gathering of young leaves, resulting in fine and tender tea with excellent quality. Since the spring tea season opened in Shanghai, sales have reached nearly 50,000 chests. The high prices and rapid sales are unprecedented. Currently, Qimen Zi tea, according to letters from Qimen estates, is entering the market. However, due to many estates selecting high-grade, tender leaves, production is greatly reduced. The opening price at the mountain is 60 yuan per dan, continuing to surge to over 100 yuan. With demand exceeding supply, the rising trend seems unstoppable. Recently, the first batches from estates such as Qicheng Jun Da, Zhangcun Fushengchang, Tafang Tongda Xin, Tongyichang, and Penglong Yida have been prepared and will be shipped soon.

According to estimates by general tea merchants, the output of Qimen Zi tea is only about 20% of last year's. The future cost of processed tea is estimated to be around 180-190 taels, it is said.

Grain: Rainy Weather Prevents River Cargo from Being Unloaded 133

▲Xin Zha Due to yesterday's rain, river cargo could not be unloaded. Only four firms, Tong Xing Gong, Wan Sheng Tai, He Feng Tai, and Heng Xing, conducted some business. Thick japonica rice, thin indica rice, and early rice all rose by a few cents. Due to shallow water in the Xiang Road waterway, vessels in the Yejidun area cannot enter. Buyers are taking advantage of the approaching holiday to push prices up. Inland sources are scarce, and market sentiment is tense. Very little Anhui and Jiangxi rice has arrived recently. Local transactions are limited, and buyers are stirring slightly, tightening the situation. A survey of rice boats along the Suzhou River yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM counted over 300 boats, holding approximately 32,000 shi of rice.

▲South Shanghai The Feng Ji wharf rice market in South Shanghai saw very few people present at the morning market. There was little interest in goods displayed for inspection. Due to the continuous rain, no river cargo was transacted, so there was no market report. Six boats from the western routes, including Jiaoli, Songjiang, Fengjing, Tongli, Jinze, and Xitang, did not unload rice due to the approaching Dragon Boat Festival and the period for settling accounts for firms.

Metals: New Stock of 3'7" East Iron Arrives 134

According to news from foreign firms yesterday, Mitsubishi Corporation, Huishanzhan, and others have received new shipments of 3'7" East White Iron, which had been in short supply for many days. Therefore, there is no concern about market shortages. The market price is 1 tael 3 mace per sheet, a slight decrease of 1 cent compared to before, it is said.

Metal Market Affected by Moldy Rain 135

Yesterday's metal trading was significantly dampened by the moldy rain, so actual transactions in the market were quite subdued. Sales were minimal except for some decorative items. However, there was strong interest in Black Iron Sheet and Huisi Iron, which had been neglected for a long time, resulting in transactions of several hundred dan each. Prices were 11 taels 7 mace 5 candareens per dan for Black Iron Sheet and 33 taels 5 mace for Huisi Iron. It is reported that buyers in Tianjin, Yantai, Qingdao, and other areas are also considering purchases.

Sugar Market: Local Refinery Raises Ice Sugar Price by 2 Mace 136

Yesterday, a telegram from the sugar producing area stated that the spot price of Cuban sugar was still 1.3125, and the price of New York sugar futures for September was 1.27, a decrease of 2 points from the previous telegram; December was 1.36, March next year was 1.44, and May was 1.50, also each down 1 point from before. The price of Java sugar futures remained unchanged. There were very few transactions in the Exchange market. Dutch No. 20 coarse granulated white sugar was offered at 11 taels 7 mace, with sluggish demand. The price of Dutch No. 20 medium granulated white sugar rose slightly in the market to 11 taels 1 mace, with a firm trend. Transactions in Japanese sugar were quiet, with the market appearing stable. Z Mark: 11 taels 3 mace 2.5 candareens. SH Mark: 11 taels 1 mace 2.5 candareens. TM Mark: 11 taels 2 mace. TX Mark: 11 taels 6 mace. AE Mark: 11 taels 7 mace.
